2:30:2053:0:14:71:226:708:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:C:Systemic Risk and Hedge Funds
2:31:2082:14:14:71:405:694:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:C:Nicholas Chan, Mila Getmansky, Shane M. Haas, and Andrew W. Lo
2:32:2144:14:14:71:232:680:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:C:NBER Working Paper No. 11200
2:33:2172:14:14:71:129:666:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:C:March 2005
2:34:2182:14:29:71:134:652:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:C:JEL No. G12
2:35:2193:29:31:273:338:623:12:g_d0_f2:12:g_d0_f2:?:ABSTRACT
2:36:2201:31:23:71:539:592:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:F:Systemic risk is commonly used to describe the possibility of a series of correlated defaults among
2:37:2300:23:22:71:539:569:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:F:financial institutions---typically banks---that occur over a short period of time, often caused by a
2:38:2400:22:23:71:539:547:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:F:single major event. However, since the collapse of Long Term Capital Management in 1998, it has
2:39:2495:23:23:71:539:524:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:F:become clear that hedge funds are also involved in systemic risk exposures. The hedge-fund industry
2:40:2594:23:22:71:539:501:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:F:has  a  symbiotic  relationship  with  the  banking  sector,  and  many  banks  now  operate  proprietary
2:41:2699:22:23:71:539:479:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:F:trading units that are organized much like hedge funds. As a result, the risk exposures of the hedge-
2:42:2800:23:23:71:539:456:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:F:fund industry may have a material impact on the banking sector, resulting in new sources of systemic
2:43:2900:23:23:71:539:433:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:F:risks. In this paper, we attempt to quantify the potential impact of hedge funds on systemic risk by
2:44:3000:23:22:71:539:410:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:F:developing a number of new risk measures for hedge funds and applying them to individual and
2:45:3092:22:25:71:539:388:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:F:aggregate hedge-fund returns data. These measures include: illiquidity risk exposure, nonlinear factor
2:46:3194:25:27:71:539:363:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:F:models  for  hedge-fund  and  banking-sector  indexes,  logistic  regression  analysis  of  hedge-fund
2:47:3296:27:27:71:539:336:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:F:liquidation probabilities, and aggregate measures of volatility and distress based on regime-switching
2:48:3398:27:27:71:539:309:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:F:models.  Our  preliminary  findings  suggest  that  the  hedge-fund  industry  may  be  heading  into  a
2:49:3502:27:32:71:508:282:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:C:challenging period of lower expected returns, and that systemic risk is currently on the rise.
2:50:3596:32:16:71:142:250:12:g_d0_f1:12:g_d0_f1:C:Nicholas Chan
